\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Canonical n-dimensional unit of homogeneous dtype contained in a pandas
data structure

Index-ignorant; let the container take care of that
\end{DoxyVerb}

 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpandas_1_1core_1_1internals_1_1blocks_1_1Block}{Block}} pandas.\+core.\+internals.\+blocks.\+Block.\+astype (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Dtype\+Obj}]{dtype}{, }\item[{bool }]{copy}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{Ignore\+Raise }]{errors}{ = {\ttfamily "{}raise"{}}, }\item[{bool }]{using\+\_\+cow}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{bool }]{squeeze}{ = {\ttfamily False}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Coerce to the new dtype.

Parameters
----------
dtype : np.dtype or ExtensionDtype
copy : bool, default False
    copy if indicated
errors : str, {'raise', 'ignore'}, default 'raise'
    - ``raise`` : allow exceptions to be raised
    - ``ignore`` : suppress exceptions. On error return original object
using_cow: bool, default False
    Signaling if copy on write copy logic is used.
squeeze : bool, default False
    squeeze values to ndim=1 if only one column is given

Returns
-------
Block
\end{DoxyVerb}

 list\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classpandas_1_1core_1_1internals_1_1blocks_1_1Block}{Block}}\mbox{]} pandas.\+core.\+internals.\+blocks.\+Block.\+delete (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{loc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Deletes the locs from the block.

We split the block to avoid copying the underlying data. We create new
blocks for every connected segment of the initial block that is not deleted.
The new blocks point to the initial array.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_inplace()}{set\_inplace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpandas_1_1core_1_1internals_1_1blocks_1_1Block_a60f222a401929c2b8a827c242e834789} 
 None pandas.\+core.\+internals.\+blocks.\+Block.\+set\+\_\+inplace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{locs}{, }\item[{Array\+Like}]{values}{, }\item[{bool }]{copy}{ = {\ttfamily False}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Modify block values in-place with new item value.

If copy=True, first copy the underlying values in place before modifying
(for Copy-on-Write).

Notes
-----
`set_inplace` never creates a new array or new Block, whereas `setitem`
_may_ create a new array and always creates a new Block.

Caller is responsible for checking values.dtype == self.dtype.
\end{DoxyVerb}
